# Grounding-Evidence Catalog

Generated by `scripts/build-evidence.ts`. The factual spine of the Morphe composer:
every capability cites a REAL endpoint + REAL compiled-model name — not a claim, an
artifact you can verify. Operations are grouped by tag; `→` marks the bound model.

## dkPlus

Spec: 2.0 · 306 operations · 261 models · `/home/rationallyprime/projects/mcp-registry/dk-mcp/openapi/dkplus_swagger_2_0.json`

### Company

- `GET /api/v1/company` — Get company related information and settings (Company_GetCompanySettings) → `dkCloud.Data.Model.Settings.SettingsModel`
- `POST /api/v1/company/action` — This action calles dk and performs a action directly in the dkERP (Company_PerformCompanyAction) → `dkPlus.API.Models.InvokeActionRequest`
- `GET /api/v1/company/connection` — Test connection to dk Data (Company_GetTestConnection)
- `GET /api/v1/company/licence` — Get Licence information (Company_GetCompanyLicence) → `dkCloud.Data.Model.Licence.Licence`
- `GET /api/v1/company/status` — (no summary) (Company_GetCompanyStatus) → `dkPlus.API.Models.CompanyStatusResponse`
- `PUT /api/v1/company/sync` — Initiliza a company sync (Company_RunCompanySync)
